<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="English">English</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=on&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: English">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronunciation">Pronunciation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=on&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Pronunciation">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">British Isles<span class="ib-comma qualifier-comma">,</span> Eastern New England</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <a href="/wiki/Appendix:English_pronunciation" title="Appendix:English pronunciation">enPR</a>: <span class="AHD enPR">ŏn</span>, <a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:International_Phonetic_Alphabet" title="Wiktionary:International Phonetic Alphabet">IPA</a><sup>(<a href="/wiki/Appendix:English_pronunciation" title="Appendix:English pronunciation">key</a>)</sup>:&#32;<span class="IPA">/ɒn/</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">Northern US<span class="ib-comma qualifier-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Cot%E2%80%93caught_merger" class="extiw" title="w:Cot–caught merger"><i>cot</i>–<i>caught</i> merger</a></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <a href="/wiki/Appendix:English_pronunciation" title="Appendix:English pronunciation">enPR</a>: <span class="AHD enPR">än</span>, <a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:International_Phonetic_Alphabet" title="Wiktionary:International Phonetic Alphabet">IPA</a><sup>(<a href="/wiki/Appendix:English_pronunciation" title="Appendix:English pronunciation">key</a>)</sup>:&#32;<span class="IPA">/ɑn/</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Southern_American_English" class="extiw" title="w:Southern American English">Southern American English</a></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:International_Phonetic_Alphabet" title="Wiktionary:International Phonetic Alphabet">IPA</a><sup>(<a href="/wiki/Appendix:English_pronunciation" title="Appendix:English pronunciation">key</a>)</sup>:&#32;<span class="IPA">/ɔn/</span></li>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=on&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Etymology 1">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href="/wiki/on#Middle_English" title="on">on</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang"><a href="/wiki/on#Old_English" title="on">on</a></i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang"><a href="/wiki/an#Old_English" title="an">an</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">on, upon, onto, in, into</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro"><a href="/wiki/Reconstruction:Proto-Germanic/ana" class="mw-redirect" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Germanic/ana">*ana</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">on, at</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro"><a href="/wiki/Reconstruction:Proto-Indo-European/h%E2%82%82en-" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Indo-European/h₂en-">*h₂en-</a></i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/North_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:North Frisian language">North Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frr"><a href="/wiki/a#North_Frisian" title="a">a</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">on, in</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Saterland_Frisian" class="extiw" title="w:Saterland Frisian">Saterland Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="stq"><a href="/wiki/an#Saterland_Frisian" title="an">an</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">on, at</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy"><a href="/wiki/oan#West_Frisian" title="oan">oan</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">on, at</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href="/wiki/aan#Dutch" title="aan">aan</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">on, at, to</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds"><a href="/wiki/an#Low_German" title="an">an</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">on, at</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv"><a href="/wiki/%C3%A5#Swedish" title="å">å</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Albanian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Albanian language">Albanian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sq"><a <h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=on&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Adjective">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en">on</strong> (<i>not <a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#comparable" title="Appendix:Glossary">comparable</a></i>)
</p>
<ol><li>In the state of being <a href="/wiki/active" title="active">active</a>, <a href="/wiki/function" title="function">functioning</a> or <a href="/wiki/operate" title="operate">operating</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/perform" title="perform">Performing</a> according to <a href="/wiki/schedule" title="schedule">schedule</a>; taking place.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">Are we still <b>on</b> for tonight?</i></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">Is the show still <b>on</b>?</i></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">We had to ration our food because there was a war <b>on</b>.</i></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">chiefly&#32;<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Britain" class="extiw" title="w:Great Britain">Britain</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span>&#32;<a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#informal" title="Appendix:Glossary">informal</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span>&#32;usually negative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Acceptable, appropriate.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">You can't do that; it's just not <b>on</b>.</i></div></dd></dl>
<ul><li><b>1998</b> May 22, "Phoenix Gamma", <i>If I was owned Nintendo...</i>, <tt>alt.games.video.nintendo-64</tt>:
<dl><dd>This kind of over-packaging of goods is completely not <b>on</b>.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>2003</b> August 12, "DAB sounds worse than FM", <i>Gerg Dyke's Speech at Radio Festival</i>, <tt>alt.radio.digital</tt>:
<dl><dd>so Simon Nelson saying on Feedback "we'd prefer it if everybody listened to digital radio via DAB" is completely not <b>on</b> at all.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#informal" title="Appendix:Glossary">informal</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href="/wiki/destined" title="destined">Destined</a>, normally in the context of a <a href="/wiki/challenge" title="challenge">challenge</a> being accepted; <a href="/wiki/involved" title="involved">involved</a>, <a href="/wiki/doomed" title="doomed">doomed</a>.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">"Five bucks says the Cavs win tonight." ―"You're <b>on</b>!"</i></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">Mike just threw coffee onto Paul's lap. It's <b>on</b> now.</i></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/baseball" title="baseball">baseball</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span>&#32;<a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#informal" title="Appendix:Glossary">informal</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Having reached a <a href="/wiki/base" title="base">base</a> as a <a href="/wiki/runner" title="runner">runner</a> and being positioned there, awaiting further action from a subsequent batter.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2019</b> February 24,  Chris Kennedy,  “Aggies Earn Series Win Over Yale in Sunday Finale”, in  <cite>New Mexico State University Athletics</cite>&#8206;<sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://nmstatesports.com/news/2019/2/24/baseball-aggies-earn-series-win-over-yale-in-sunday-finale.aspx">[1]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">With one out and no men <b>on</b>, Tristen Carranza belted a ball to the opposite field for a solo home run to put the NM State deficit at just 2-1.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2019</b> April 6,  Daniel Martinez-Krams,  “Baseball Falls Short in Game 2 of UCLA Series”, in  <cite>The Stanford Daily</cite>&#8206;<sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://www.stanforddaily.com/2019/04/06/baseball-falls-short-in-game-2-of-ucla-series/">[2]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Although Stanford was outhit 15-6, the Cardinal stranded eight runners to UCLA's three, hitting just 3-15 with runners <b>on</b> compared to the Bruin's 9-22.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#euphemism" title="Appendix:Glossary">euphemistic</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href="/wiki/menstruating" title="menstruating">Menstruating</a>.
<ul><li><b>2011</b>, Netmums, Hollie Smith, <i>You and Your Tween: Managing the years from 9 to 13</i>, Hachette UK <a href="/wiki/Special:BookSources/9780755361137" title="Special:BookSources/9780755361137">→ISBN</a>
<dl><dd>It still gets in the way of her doing things like swimming, and she avoids sleepovers when she&#39;s &#39;<b>on</b>&#39;.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>

<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">baseball: positioned at a base</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">on</span> <a href="/wiki/base" title="base">base</a> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">not informal</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ul>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=on&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: Adverb">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en">on</strong> (<i>not <a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#comparable" title="Appendix:Glossary">comparable</a></i>)
</p>
<ol><li>To an <a href="/wiki/operate" title="operate">operating</a> <a href="/wiki/state" title="state">state</a>.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">turn the <a href="/wiki/television#English" title="television">television</a> <b>on</b></i></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>Along, forwards (continuing an action).
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">drive <b>on</b>, rock <b>on</b></i></div></dd></dl>
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2012</b> May 5,  Phil McNulty,  “Chelsea 2-1 Liverpool”, in  <cite>BBC Sport</cite>&#8206;<sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/sport/0/football/17878435">[3]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">He met Luis Suarez's cross at the far post, only for Chelsea keeper Petr Cech to show brilliant reflexes to deflect his header on to the bar. Carroll turned away to lead Liverpool's insistent protests that the ball had crossed the line but referee Phil Dowd and assistant referee Andrew Garratt waved play <b>on</b>, with even a succession of replays proving inconclusive.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li>In continuation, at length.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">and so <b>on</b>.</i></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">He rambled <b>on</b> and <b>on</b>.</i></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/cricket" title="cricket">cricket</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> In, or towards the <a href="/wiki/half" title="half">half</a> of the <a href="/wiki/field" title="field">field</a> on the same side as the <a href="/wiki/batsman" title="batsman">batsman</a>'s <a href="/wiki/leg" title="leg">legs</a>; the <a href="/wiki/left" title="left">left</a> side for a <a href="/wiki/right-handed" title="right-handed">right-handed</a> batsman; <a href="/wiki/leg" title="leg">leg</a>. <span class="maintenance-line" style="color: #777777;">(Can we add an <a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:Example_sentences" title="Wiktionary:Example sentences">example</a> for this sense?)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete in the US</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href="/wiki/later" title="later">Later</a>.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">Ten years <b>on</b>, nothing had changed in the village.</i></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="use-with-mention">Of betting odds, denoting a better than even chance.</span> <i>See also </i><b><a href="/wiki/odds-on" title="odds-on">odds-on</a></b><i>.</i>
<dl><dd><i>That horse is at twenty-to-one <b>on</b>, so you need to stake twenty pounds just to win one pound.</i></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Antonyms">Antonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=on&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: Antonyms">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">active, functioning, operating</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/off#English" title="off">off</a></span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">to an operating state</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/off#English" title="off">off</a></span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">later</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/after#English" title="after">after</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/afterward#English" title="afterward">afterward</a></span>/<a href="/wiki/afterwards" title="afterwards">afterwards</a>, <a href="/wiki/later" title="later">later</a>, <a href="/wiki/subsequently" title="subsequently">subsequently</a>, <a href="/wiki/thence" title="thence">thence</a></li></ul>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Preposition">Preposition</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=on&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: Preposition">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Encima.png" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3a/Encima.png/220px-Encima.png" decoding="async" width="220" height="157" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3a/Encima.png/330px-Encima.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/3/3a/Encima.png 2x" data-file-width="420" data-file-height="300" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Encima.png" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>A green pepper <b>on</b> (positioned on the upper surface of) a box</div></div></div>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en">on</strong>
</p>
<ol><li>Positioned at the <a href="/wiki/upper" title="upper">upper</a> surface of, <a href="/wiki/touch" title="touch">touching</a> from <a href="/wiki/above" title="above">above</a>.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en"><b>on</b> the table;&#160; <b>on</b> the couch</i></div></dd>
<dd><i>The parrot was sitting <b>on</b> Jim's shoulder.</i></dd></dl>
<ul><li><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: #777777;">(Can we <a href="/wiki/Category:Requests_for_date" title="Category:Requests for date">date</a> this quote by Longfellow and provide title, author's full name, and other details?)</span>
<dl><dd>I stood <b>on</b> the bridge at midnight.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li>At or near; adjacent to.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">Soon we'll pass a statue <b>on</b> the left.</i></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">The fleet is <b>on</b> the American coast.</i></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Croton-on-Hudson" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Croton-on-Hudson">Croton<b>-on-</b>Hudson</a>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Rostov-on-Don" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Rostov-on-Don">Rostov<b>-on-</b>Don</a>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Southend-on-Sea" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Southend-on-Sea">Southend<b>-on-</b>Sea</a></i></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/covering" title="covering">Covering</a>.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">He wore old shoes <b>on</b> his feet.</i></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>At the <a href="/wiki/date" title="date">date</a> of.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">Born <b>on</b> the 4th of July.</i></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>Some time during the <a href="/wiki/day" title="day">day</a> of.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">I'll see you <b>on</b> Monday.&#8195; The bus leaves <b>on</b> Friday.&#8195; Can I see you <b>on</b> a different day? <b>On</b> Sunday I'm busy.</i></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/deal" title="deal">Dealing</a> with the <a href="/wiki/subject" title="subject">subject</a> of, about, or concerning something.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">A book <b>on</b> history.&#8195; The World Summit <b>on</b> the Information Society.</i></div></dd></dl>
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1869</b> May,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Anthony_Trollope" class="extiw" title="w:Anthony Trollope">Anthony Trollope</a>,  “Lady Milborough as Ambassador”, in  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/He_Knew_He_Was_Right" class="extiw" title="w:He Knew He Was Right">He Knew He Was Right</a></cite>, volume I, London&#58; Strahan and Company, publishers,<span class="q-hellip-sp">&#160;</span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span><span title="56, Ludgate Hill, London">…</span><span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"></span>, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OCLC" class="extiw" title="w:OCLC">OCLC</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://worldcat.org/oclc/1118026626">1118026626</a></small>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://books.google.com/books?id=Sb4BAAAAQAAJ&amp;pg=PA85">page 85</a>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">[...] I received a note from that gentleman <b>on</b> a most trivial matter. I answered it as trivially.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/touch" title="touch">Touching</a>; <a href="/wiki/hang" title="hang">hanging</a> from.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">The fruit ripened <b>on</b> the trees.&#8195; The painting hangs <b>on</b> the wall.</i></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#informal" title="Appendix:Glossary">informal</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> In the possession of.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">I haven't got any money <b>on</b> me.</i></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>Because of, or due to.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">To arrest someone <b>on</b> suspicion of bribery.&#8195; To contact someone <b>on</b> a hunch.</i></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/upon" title="upon">Upon</a>; at the time of (and often because of).
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en"><b>On</b> Jack's entry, William got up to leave.</i></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en"><b>On</b> the addition of ammonia, a chemical reaction begins.</i></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>Paid for by.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">The drinks are <b>on</b> me tonight, boys.&#8195; The meal is <b>on</b> the house.&#8195; I paid for the airfare and meals for my family, but the hotel room was <b>on</b> the company.</i></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="use-with-mention">Used to indicate a means or medium.</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">I saw it <b>on</b> television.&#8195; Can't you see I'm <b>on</b> the phone?&#8195; My favorite shows are <b>on</b> BBC America.&#8195; The Beatles appearance <b>on</b> the <i>Ed Sullivan Show</i> is <b>on</b> YouTube.&#8195; The film was released <b>on</b> DVD.</i></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="use-with-mention">Indicating a means of subsistence.</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">They lived <b>on</b> ten dollars a week.&#8195; The dog survived three weeks <b>on</b> rainwater.</i></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>Away or occupied with (e.g. a scheduled activity).
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">He's <b>on</b> his lunch break.&#8195; <b>on</b> vacation;&#160; <b>on</b> holiday</i></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>Denoting performance or action by contact with the surface, upper part, or outside of anything; hence, by means of; with.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">to play <b>on</b> a violin or piano</i></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">Her words made a lasting impression <b>on</b> my mind.</i></div></dd></dl></li>
<li class="mw-empty-elt"></li><li class="senseid" id="English-a_drug"> Regularly taking (a drug).
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">You've been <b>on</b> these antidepressants far too long.&#8195; He's acting so strangely, I think he must be <b>on</b> something.</i></div></dd></dl></li>
<li class="mw-empty-elt"></li><li class="senseid" id="English-influenced_by_a_drug"> Under the influence of (a drug).
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">He's acting crazy because he's <b>on</b> crack right now.</i></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/mathematics" title="mathematics">mathematics</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Having identical <a href="/wiki/domain" title="domain">domain</a> and <a href="/wiki/codomain" title="codomain">codomain</a>.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">a function <b>on</b></i></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/mathematics" title="mathematics">mathematics</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Having <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle V^{n}}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <msup>
          <mi>V</mi>
          <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
            <mi>n</mi>
          </mrow>
        </msup>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle V^{n}}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/cbfbf91428ae481b792337be15fdae34db6331ad" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:3.135ex; height:2.343ex;" alt="V^{n}"/></span> as <a href="/wiki/domain" title="domain">domain</a> and <i>V</i> as <a href="/wiki/codomain" title="codomain">codomain</a>, for some set <i>V</i> and integer <i>n</i>.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">an operator <b>on</b></i></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/mathematics" title="mathematics">mathematics</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href="/wiki/generate" title="generate">Generated</a> by.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">the free group <b>on</b> four letters</i></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/support" title="support">Supported</a> by (the specified part of itself).
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">A table can't stand <b>on</b> two legs.&#8195; After resting <b>on</b> his elbows, he stood <b>on</b> his toes, then walked <b>on</b> his heels.</i></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>At a given time after the start of something; <a href="/wiki/at#Preposition" title="at">at</a>.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2011</b> September 24,  Aled Williams,  “<a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/sport2/hi/football/eng_prem/14957961.stm">Chelsea 4-1 Swansea</a>”, in  <cite>BBC Sport</cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">The Spain striker had given Chelsea the lead <b>on</b> 29 minutes but was shown a straight red card 10 minutes later for a rash challenge on Mark Gower.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li>In addition to; besides; indicating multiplication or succession in a series.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">heaps <b>on</b> heaps of food</i></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">mischief <b>on</b> mischief; loss <b>on</b> loss</i></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#obsolete" title="Appendix:Glossary">obsolete</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span>&#32;regional</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href="/wiki/of" title="of">of</a>
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1599</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Shakespeare" class="extiw" title="w:William Shakespeare">William Shakespeare</a>,  “<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Julius_Caesar_(play)" class="extiw" title="w:Julius Caesar (play)">The Tragedie of Ivlivs Cæsar</a>”, in  <cite>Mr. William Shakespeares Comedies, Histories, &amp; Tragedies: Published According to the True Originall Copies</cite> (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/First_Folio" class="extiw" title="w:First Folio">First Folio</a>), London&#58; Printed by <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Jaggard" class="extiw" title="w:William Jaggard">Isaac Iaggard</a>, and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Edward_Blount" class="extiw" title="w:Edward Blount">Ed[ward] Blount</a>, published 1623, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OCLC" class="extiw" title="w:OCLC">OCLC</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://worldcat.org/oclc/606515358">606515358</a></small>, [Act I, scene ii]:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Be not jealous <b>on</b> me.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><i><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#c." title="Appendix:Glossary"><abbr title="circa">c.</abbr></a></i> <b>1606</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Shakespeare" class="extiw" title="w:William Shakespeare">William Shakespeare</a>,  “<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Macbeth" class="extiw" title="w:Macbeth">The Tragedie of Macbeth</a>”, in  <cite>Mr. William Shakespeares Comedies, Histories, &amp; Tragedies: Published According to the True Originall Copies</cite> (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/First_Folio" class="extiw" title="w:First Folio">First Folio</a>), London&#58; Printed by <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Jaggard" class="extiw" title="w:William Jaggard">Isaac Iaggard</a>, and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Edward_Blount" class="extiw" title="w:Edward Blount">Ed[ward] Blount</a>, published 1623, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OCLC" class="extiw" title="w:OCLC">OCLC</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://worldcat.org/oclc/606515358">606515358</a></small>, [Act I, scene iii]:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Or have we eaten <b>on</b> the insane root / That takes the reason prisoner?</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li>Indicating dependence or reliance; with confidence in.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">I depended <b>on</b> them for assistance.</i></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">He will promise <b>on</b> certain conditions.</i></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">Do you ever bet <b>on</b> horses?</i></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>Toward; for; indicating the object of an emotion.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">Have pity or compassion <b>on</b> him.</i></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#obsolete" title="Appendix:Glossary">obsolete</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> At the peril of, or for the safety of.
<ul><li><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: #777777;">(Can we <a href="/wiki/Category:Requests_for_date" title="Category:Requests for date">date</a> this quote by Dryden and provide title, author's full name, and other details?)</span>
<dl><dd>Hence, <b>on</b> thy life.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li>In the service of; connected with; of the number of.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">He is <b>on</b> a newspaper; I am <b>on</b> the committee.</i></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>By virtue of; with the pledge of.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">He affirmed or promised <b>on</b> his word, or <b>on</b> his honour.</i></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>To the account or detriment of; denoting imprecation or invocation, or coming to, falling, or resting upon.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en"><b>On</b> us be all the blame.</i></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">A curse <b>on</b> him!</i></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">Please don't tell <b>on</b> her and get her in trouble.</i></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">He turned <b>on</b> her and has been her enemy ever since.</i></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">He went all honest <b>on</b> me, making me listen to his confession.</i></div></dd></dl>
<ul><li>Bible, Matthew xxvii. 25
<dl><dd>His blood be <b>on</b> us and <b>on</b> our children.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">especially when numbers of combatants or competitors are specified</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Against; in opposition to.
<dl><dd><i>The fight was three <b>on</b> one, and he never stood a chance.</i></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms_2">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=on&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: Synonyms">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">dealing with the subject of</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/about#English" title="about">about</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/apropos#English" title="apropos">apropos</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/as_for#English" title="as for">as for</a></span>; See also <a href="/wiki/Thesaurus:about" title="Thesaurus:about">Thesaurus:about</a></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">because of</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/by_dint_of#English" title="by dint of">by dint of</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/due_to#English" title="due to">due to</a></span>; See also <a href="/wiki/Thesaurus:because_of" title="Thesaurus:because of">Thesaurus:because of</a></li></ul>

<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Translations_3">Translations</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=on&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: Translations">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=on&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: Verb">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en">on</strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3&#124;s&#124;pres-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/ons#English" title="ons">ons</a></b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres&#124;ptcp-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/oning#English" title="oning">oning</a></b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past&#124;and&#124;past&#124;ptcp-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/oned#English" title="oned">oned</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#transitive" title="Appendix:Glossary">transitive</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span>&#32;<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Singapore" class="extiw" title="w:Singapore">Singapore</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span>&#32;<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Philippines" class="extiw" title="w:Philippines">Philippines</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to <a href="/wiki/switch" title="switch">switch</a> on
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">Can you <b>on</b> the light?</i></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/turn_on#English" title="turn on">turn on</a></span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=on&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: Etymology 2">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old Norse</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non"><a href="/wiki/%C3%B3n#Old_Norse" title="ón">ón</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="non"><a href="/wiki/%C3%A1n#Old_Norse" title="án">án</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">without</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro"><a href="/wiki/Reconstruction:Proto-Germanic/%C4%93nu" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Germanic/ēnu">*ēnu</a></i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro"><a href="/w/index.php?title=Reconstruction:Proto-Germanic/%C4%93no&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Germanic/ēno (page does not exist)">*ēno</a></i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro"><a href="/w/index.php?title=Reconstruction:Proto-Germanic/ino&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Germanic/ino (page does not exist)">*ino</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">without</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro"><a href="/w/index.php?title=Reconstruction:Proto-Indo-European/anew&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Indo-European/anew (page does not exist)">*anew</a></i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro"><a href="/w/index.php?title=Reconstruction:Proto-Indo-European/enew&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Indo-European/enew (page does not exist)">*enew</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">without</span><span Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/North_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:North Frisian language">North Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href="/wiki/an#Middle_Dutch" title="an">an</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href="/wiki/on#Middle_Dutch" title="on">on</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">without</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German">Middle Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml"><a <h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Preposition_2">Preposition</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=on&amp;action=edit&amp;section=19" title="Edit section: Preposition">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Britain" class="extiw" title="w:Great Britain">Britain</a>&#32;&#32;<a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#dialectal" title="Appendix:Glossary">dialectal</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span>&#32;<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Scotland" class="extiw" title="w:Scotland">Scotland</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href="/wiki/without" title="without">Without</a>.</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=on&amp;action=edit&amp;section=20" title="Edit section: Usage notes">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>
<ul><li>Usually followed by a present participle, as <i>being</i>, <i>having</i>, etc.</li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=on&amp;action=edit&amp;section=21" title="Edit section: Etymology 3">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Japanese_language" class="extiw" title="w:Japanese language">Japanese</a></span> <i class="Jpan mention" lang="ja"><a href="/wiki/%E9%9F%B3%E8%AA%AD%E3%81%BF#Japanese" title="音読み">音読み</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-tr tr">on-yomi</span>, literally <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">sound reading</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=on&amp;action=edit&amp;section=22" title="Edit section: Noun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en">on</strong>
</p>
<ol><li>In the Japanese language, a pronunciation, or reading, of a <a href="/wiki/kanji" title="kanji">kanji</a> character that was originally based on the character's pronunciation in Chinese, contrasted with <a href="/wiki/kun" title="kun">kun</a>.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">Most kanji have two kinds of reading, called "on" and "kun".</i></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=on&amp;action=edit&amp;section=25" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Turkic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Turkic language">Proto-Turkic</a></span></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="trk-pro"><a href="/w/index.php?title=Reconstruction:Proto-Turkic/%C5%8Dn&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Turkic/ōn (page does not exist)">*ōn</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">ten</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Turkic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Old Turkic language">Old Turkic</a></span> <small>[Term?]</small> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="ts mention-ts Latn">/on/</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">ten</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Catalan">Catalan</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=on&amp;action=edit&amp;section=30" title="Edit section: Catalan">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Alternative_forms_2">Alternative forms</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=on&amp;action=edit&amp;section=31" title="Edit section: Alternative forms">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="ca"><a href="/wiki/ahont#Catalan" title="ahont">ahont</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="ca"><a href="/wiki/hon#Catalan" title="hon">hon</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="ca"><a href="/wiki/hont#Catalan" title="hont">hont</a></span> (<i>archaic</i>)</li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_5">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=on&amp;action=edit&amp;section=32" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Occitan" class="extiw" title="w:Old Occitan">Old Occitan</a></span> <small>[Term?]</small> (compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Occitan_language" class="extiw" title="w:Occitan language">Occitan</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="oc"><a href="/wiki/ont#Occitan" title="ont">ont</a></i>), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href="/wiki/unde#Latin" title="unde">unde</a></i> (compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href="/wiki/dont#French" title="dont">dont</a></i>).
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronunciation_2">Pronunciation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=on&amp;action=edit&amp;section=33" title="Edit section: Pronunciation">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Balearic_dialect" class="extiw" title="w:Balearic dialect">Balearic</a><span class="ib-comma qualifier-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Central_Catalan" class="extiw" title="w:Central Catalan">Central</a><span class="ib-comma qualifier-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Valencian" class="extiw" title="w:Valencian">Valencian</a></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:International_Phonetic_Alphabet" title="Wiktionary:International Phonetic Alphabet">IPA</a><sup>(<a href="/wiki/Appendix:Catalan_pronunciation" title="Appendix:Catalan pronunciation">key</a>)</sup>:&#32;<span class="IPA">/ˈon/</span></li></ul>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Central_Franconian">Central Franconian</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=on&amp;action=edit&amp;section=36" title="Edit section: Central Franconian">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Alternative_forms_3">Alternative forms</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=on&amp;action=edit&amp;section=37" title="Edit section: Alternative forms">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="gmw-cfr"><a href="/wiki/un#Central_Franconian" title="un">un</a></span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">widely in free variation</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="gmw-cfr"><a href="/wiki/en#Central_Franconian" title="en">en</a></span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">some western dialects</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_6">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=on&amp;action=edit&amp;section=38" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The native form in most dialects was <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh"><a href="/wiki/indi#Old_High_German" title="indi">indi</a></i>, whence the variant <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmw-cfr">en</i>. In parts of the Eifel, this <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">indi</i> regularly becomes <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmw-cfr">on</i> (compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Luxembourgish" class="extiw" title="w:Luxembourgish">Luxembourgish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lb"><a href="/wiki/an#Luxembourgish" title="an">an</a></i>). In southern and eastern dialects, on the other hand, <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmw-cfr">on</i> may have been inherited from the Old High German variant <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh"><a href="/wiki/unde#Old_High_German" title="unde">unde</a></i> (<i class="Latn mention" lang="goh"><a href="/wiki/unti#Old_High_German" title="unti">unti</a></i>). From these two groups of dialects, the form will have spread, without doubt under influence of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href="/wiki/und#German" title="und">und</a></i>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronunciation_3">Pronunciation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=on&amp;action=edit&amp;section=39" title="Edit section: Pronunciation">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:International_Phonetic_Alphabet" title="Wiktionary:International Phonetic Alphabet">IPA</a><sup>(<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Central_Franconian_phonology" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Central Franconian phonology">key</a>)</sup>:&#32;<span class="IPA">/on/</span></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Conjunction">Conjunction</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=on&amp;action=edit&amp;section=40" title="Edit section: Conjunction">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="gmw-cfr">on</strong>
</p>
<ol><li><a href="/wiki/and" title="and">and</a>
<dl><dd><i>Salz <b>on</b> Päfer</i>
<dl><dd>salt <b>and</b> pepper</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr />

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Cornish">Cornish</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=on&amp;action=edit&amp;section=45" title="Edit section: Cornish">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Alternative_forms_4">Alternative forms</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=on&amp;action=edit&amp;section=46" title="Edit section: Alternative forms">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_7">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=on&amp;action=edit&amp;section=47" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Celtic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Celtic language">Proto-Celtic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="cel-pro"><a href="/w/index.php?title=Reconstruction:Proto-Celtic/ognos&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Celtic/ognos (page does not exist)">*ognos</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro"><a href="/wiki/Reconstruction:Proto-Indo-European/h%E2%82%82eg%CA%B7n%C3%B3s" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Indo-European/h₂egʷnós">*h₂egʷnós</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">lamb</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Czech">Czech</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=on&amp;action=edit&amp;section=52" title="Edit section: Czech">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_8">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=on&amp;action=edit&amp;section=53" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro"><a href="/wiki/Reconstruction:Proto-Slavic/on%D1%8A" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Slavic/onъ">*onъ</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro"><a href="/w/index.php?title=Reconstruction:Proto-Indo-European/h%E2%82%82eno-&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Indo-European/h₂eno- (page does not exist)">*h₂eno-</a></i>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronunciation_5">Pronunciation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=on&amp;action=edit&amp;section=54" title="Edit section: Pronunciation">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb_3">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=on&amp;action=edit&amp;section=60" title="Edit section: Adverb">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl">on</strong>
</p>
<ol><li>rarely used as shorthand for <a href="/wiki/oneven" title="oneven">oneven</a> (<a href="/wiki/odd" title="odd">odd</a>), the prefix <a href="/wiki/on-" title="on-">on-</a> means <i>not</i> (corresponds to English <a href="/wiki/un-" title="un-">un-</a>)</li></ol>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="French">French</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=on&amp;action=edit&amp;section=68" title="Edit section: French">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Alternative_forms_5">Alternative forms</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=on&amp;action=edit&amp;section=69" title="Edit section: Alternative forms">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="fr"><a href="/wiki/l%27on#French" title="l&#39;on">l'on</a></span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">formal</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_9">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=on&amp;action=edit&amp;section=70" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a href="/wiki/hom#Old_French" title="hom">hom</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a href="/wiki/om#Old_French" title="om">om</a></i> (nominative form), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href="/wiki/homo#Latin" title="homo">homō</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">human being</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (compare <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href="/wiki/homme#French" title="homme">homme</a></i> from the Old French oblique form <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a href="/wiki/home#Old_French" title="home">home</a></i>, from the Latin accusative form <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href="/wiki/hominem#Latin" title="hominem">hominem</a></i>). Its pronominal use is of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Germanic_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Germanic languages">Germanic</a></span> origin. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang"><a href="/wiki/man#Old_English" title="man">man</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">one, they, people</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, reduced form of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang"><a href="/wiki/mann#Old_English" title="mann">mann</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">man, person</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Catalan_language" class="extiw" title="w:Catalan language">Catalan</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="ca"><a href="/wiki/hom#Catalan" title="hom">hom</a></i>; <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href="/wiki/man#German" title="man">man</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">one, they, people</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href="/wiki/men#Dutch" title="men">men</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">one, they, people</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronunciation_8">Pronunciation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=on&amp;action=edit&amp;section=71" title="Edit section: Pronunciation">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:International_Phonetic_Alphabet" title="Wiktionary:International Phonetic Alphabet">IPA</a><sup>(<a href="/wiki/Appendix:French_pronunciation" title="Appendix:French pronunciation">key</a>)</sup>:&#32;<span class="IPA">/ɔ̃/</span></li>
<li><link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r50165410"/><table class="audiotable" style="vertical-align: bottom; display:inline-block; list-style:none;line-height: 1em; border-collapse:collapse;"><tbody><tr><td class="unicode audiolink" style="padding-right:5px; padding-left: 0;">audio</td><td class="audiofile"><div class="mediaContainer" style="width:175px"><audio id="mwe_player_4" controls="" preload="none" style="width:175px" class="kskin" data-durationhint="0.85" data-startoffset="0" data-mwtitle="Fr-on.ogg" data-mwprovider="wikimediacommons"><source src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/3/38/Fr-on.ogg" type="audio/ogg; codecs=&quot;vorbis&quot;" data-title="Original Ogg file (112 kbps)" data-shorttitle="Ogg source" data-width="0" data-height="0" data-bandwidth="111802" /><source src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/transcoded/3/38/Fr-on.ogg/Fr-on.ogg.mp3" type="audio/mpeg" data-title="MP3" data-shorttitle="MP3" data-transcodekey="mp3" data-width="0" data-height="0" data-bandwidth="149616" /></audio></div></td><td class="audiometa" style="font-size: 80%;">(<a href="/wiki/File:Fr-on.ogg" title="File:Fr-on.ogg">file</a>)</td></tr></tbody></table></li>
<li><span class="homophones"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#homophone" title="Appendix:Glossary">Homophone</a>: <span class="Latn" lang="fr"><a href="/wiki/ont#French" title="ont">ont</a></span></span></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronoun_3">Pronoun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=on&amp;action=edit&amp;section=72" title="Edit section: Pronoun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="fr">on</strong>&#160;<span class="gender"><abbr title="gender incomplete">?</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">indefinite</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href="/wiki/one" title="one">one</a>, <a href="/wiki/people" title="people">people</a>, <a href="/wiki/you" title="you">you</a>, <a href="/wiki/someone" title="someone">someone</a> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">an unspecified individual</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="fr"><a href="/wiki/quelqu%27un#French" title="quelqu&#39;un">quelqu'un</a> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">in some contexts</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="fr"><a href="/wiki/l%27on#French" title="l&#39;on">l'on</a> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">formal</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></span></span></dd></dl>
<ul><li><b>2003</b>, Natasha St. Pier, <i>L’instant d’après</i> (album), <i>Quand on cherche l’amour</i> (song)
<dl><dd>Quand <b>on</b> cherche l'amour...
<dl><dd>When <b>one</b> searches for love...</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ul>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="fr"><b>On</b> ne peut pas pêcher ici</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>You</b> can’t fish here</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">personal<span class="ib-comma">,</span>&#32;<a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#informal" title="Appendix:Glossary">informal</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href="/wiki/we" title="we">we</a>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="fr"><a href="/wiki/nous#French" title="nous">nous</a> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">in some contexts</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></span></span></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="fr"><b>On</b> s’est amusés.</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>We</b> had fun.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes_2">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=on&amp;action=edit&amp;section=73" title="Edit section: Usage notes">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<ul><li>In informal French, <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href="/wiki/on#French" title="on">on</a></i> has almost completely replaced the pronoun <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href="/wiki/nous#French" title="nous">nous</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">we</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> to indicate the first person plural.</li>
<li>The variant <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href="/wiki/l%27on#French" title="l&#39;on">l'on</a></i> is used in more formal or literary contexts.</li></ul>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="German_Low_German">German Low German</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=on&amp;action=edit&amp;section=78" title="Edit section: German Low German">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Conjunction_2">Conjunction</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=on&amp;action=edit&amp;section=79" title="Edit section: Conjunction">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nds-de">on</strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">in several dialects, including&#32;&#32;<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_Prussian_dialect" class="extiw" title="w:Low Prussian dialect">Low Prussian</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">Alternative form of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Latn mention" lang="nds-de"><a href="/wiki/un#German_Low_German" title="un">un</a></i></span></span> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">and</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nds-de">Melk <b>on</b> Brot</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">milk <b>and</b> bread</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronunciation_9">Pronunciation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=on&amp;action=edit&amp;section=81" title="Edit section: Pronunciation">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronoun_4">Pronoun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=on&amp;action=edit&amp;section=82" title="Edit section: Pronoun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Serbo-Croatian">Serbo-Croatian</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=on&amp;action=edit&amp;section=142" title="Edit section: Serbo-Croatian">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_15">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=on&amp;action=edit&amp;section=143" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro"><a href="/wiki/Reconstruction:Proto-Slavic/on%D1%8A" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Slavic/onъ">*onъ</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro"><a href="/w/index.php?title=Reconstruction:Proto-Indo-European/h%E2%82%82eno-&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Indo-European/h₂eno- (page does not exist)">*h₂eno-</a></i>
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Slovak">Slovak</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=on&amp;action=edit&amp;section=148" title="Edit section: Slovak">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_16">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=on&amp;action=edit&amp;section=149" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro"><a href="/wiki/Reconstruction:Proto-Slavic/on%D1%8A" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Slavic/onъ">*onъ</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro"><a href="/w/index.php?title=Reconstruction:Proto-Indo-European/h%E2%82%82eno-&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Indo-European/h₂eno- (page does not exist)">*h₂eno-</a></i>; inflected forms from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro"><a href="/wiki/Reconstruction:Proto-Slavic/j%D1%8C" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Slavic/jь">*jь</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro"><a href="/wiki/Reconstruction:Proto-Indo-European/%C3%A9y" class="mw-redirect" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Indo-European/éy">*éy</a></i>.
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Slovene">Slovene</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=on&amp;action=edit&amp;section=154" title="Edit section: Slovene">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_17">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=on&amp;action=edit&amp;section=155" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro"><a href="/wiki/Reconstruction:Proto-Slavic/on%D1%8A" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Slavic/onъ">*onъ</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro"><a href="/w/index.php?title=Reconstruction:Proto-Indo-European/h%E2%82%82eno-&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Indo-European/h₂eno- (page does not exist)">*h₂eno-</a></i>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronunciation_15">Pronunciation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=on&amp;action=edit&amp;section=156" title="Edit section: Pronunciation">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:International_Phonetic_Alphabet" title="Wiktionary:International Phonetic Alphabet">IPA</a><sup>(<a href="/wiki/Appendix:Slovene_pronunciation" title="Appendix:Slovene pronunciation">key</a>)</sup>:&#32;<span class="IPA">/ɔ́n/</span></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronoun_13">Pronoun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=on&amp;action=edit&amp;section=157" title="Edit section: Pronoun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="sl">ȍn</strong>
</p>
<ol><li><a href="/wiki/he" title="he">he</a></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=on&amp;action=edit&amp;section=158" title="Edit section: Inflection">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Forms between parentheses indicate clitic forms; the main forms are used for emphasis.
